        "text": "All historical trades can be fetched via the Polymarket CLOB REST API. A trade is initiated by a &quot;taker&quot; who creates a marketable limit order. This limit order can be matched against one or more resting limit orders on the associated book. A trade can be in various states as described below.\n\nWelcome to the Polymarket Order Book API! In this documentation you will find overviews, explanations, examples and annotations that aim to make interacting with the order book a breeze. In this section we will provide a general overview of the Polymarket Order Book and the purpose of the API before diving deep into the API and clients in following sections. Polymarket's Order Book, also referred to as the \"CLOB\" (Central Limit Order Book) or \"BLOB\" (Binary Limit Order Book), is hybrid-decentralized wherein there is an operator that provides off-chain matching/ordering services while settlement/execution happens on-chain, non-custodially according to instructions provided by users in the form of signed order messages. This decentralized exchange model provides users with a powerful, non-custodial exchange experience. Underlying the exchange system is a custom Exchange contract that facilitates atomic swaps (settlement) between binary Outcome Tokens (both CTF ERC1155 assets and ERC20 PT\n\nReward allocations for an epoch can be fetched via the Markets API. ... All outcomes on Polymarket are tokenized on the Polygon network. Specifically, Polymarket outcome shares are binary outcomes (ie \u201cYES\u201d and \u201cNO\u201d) represented using Gnosis\u2019 Conditional Token Framework (CTF). They are distinct ERC1155 tokens related to a parent condition and backed by some collateral. More technically, the binary outcome tokens are referred to as \u201cpositionIds\u201d in Gnosis\u2019s documentation. \u201cPositionIds\u201d are derived from a collateral token and distinct \u201ccollectionIds\u201d. \u201cCollectionIds\u201d are derived from a \u201cparentCollectionId\u201d, (always bytes32(0) in our case) a \u201cconditionId\u201d, and a unique \u201cindexSet\u201d. The \u201cindexSet\u201d is a 256 bit array denoting which outcome slots are in an outcome collection; it must be a nonempty proper subset of a condition\u2019s outcome slots.\n\nThe Polymarket Order Book API is a set of endpoints that allow market makers, traders, and other Polymarket users to programmatically create and manage orders for markets via access to the API provided by the operator. Orders for any amount can be created and listed, or fetched and read from the order book for a given market. The API also provides data on all available markets, market prices, and order history through REST and WSS endpoints. Polymarket's Exchange contract has been audited by Chainsecurity you can find the audit report here. The operator has no special privileges outside of ordering, this means that the only actions you must trust them with is enforcing correct ordering, not censoring and removing cancellations (orders can also be cancelled on-chain if operator is not trusted). If the operator is not doing any of these activities fairly a user can simply stop interacting with the operator.\n\nAll historical trades can be fetched via the Polymarket CLOB REST API. A trade is initiated by a \"taker\" who creates a marketable limit order. This limit order can be matched against one or more resting limit orders on the associated book. A trade can be in various states as described below. Note in some cases (due to gas limitations) the execution of a \"trade\" must be broken into multiple transactions in which case separate trade entities will be returned. To make these trade entires associable, there is a bucket_index field, a market_order field and a match_time field. Trades that have been broken into multiple trade objects can be reconciled by combining trade objects with the same market_order, match_time and incrementing bucket_indexs into a top level \"trade\" client side. This endpoint required a L2 Header. Get trades for the authenticated user based on the provided filters.",

This paper provides a comprehensive technical overview of the latest Polymarket API (as of ...\n\nPolymarket is a decentralized prediction markets platform that enables users to trade on the outcomes of future events using blockchain technology[1]. This paper provides a comprehensive technical overview of the latest Polymarket API (as of early 2026), detailing its architecture, endpoints, and data structures in a formal documentation style. We describe how the API is organized into multiple services (notably the Gamma market data API, the CLOB trading API, and the Data API) and how each interacts with Polymarket\u2019s underlying smart contracts on the Polygon blockchain. Every publicly available REST endpoint and its fields are explicated with formal definitions, and we illustrate common usage patterns \u2014 such as fetching market listings, querying outcome prices, interpreting market liquidity, and deriving predictions from market data. Code examples in Python and JavaScript are provided to demonstrate integrating the API for tasks like retrieving markets and order books, computing proba\n\nThis paper presents a full technical overview of the Polymarket API\u2019s latest iteration. We begin with background on Polymarket\u2019s system architecture, including how on-chain conditional tokens and oracle mechanisms underpin the markets. We then describe the API architecture, explaining the separation of concerns between the Gamma API (for market metadata and discovery), the CLOB API (central limit order book for trading operations), and the Data API (for user-specific data like positions and trade history). In a formal reference-style section, we enumerate every major API endpoint and provide detailed descriptions of each field returned, effectively serving as a structured documentation of the API. Subsequently, we explore common use cases and provide annotated code examples demonstrating how to use the API for tasks such as fetching the list of active markets, querying the latest prices of outcomes, examining the liquidity and order book depth of a market, and interpreting those result\n\nWe also explain how the API\u2019s outputs relate to on-chain data \u2014 such as how an outcome\u2019s price corresponds to token swaps on the blockchain and how market resolution is achieved via the UMA Optimistic Oracle[5]. We conclude with a summary of the API\u2019s significance for developers and potential future directions. Throughout the paper, we maintain a formal tone and cite relevant documentation and sources for clarity. The aim is to provide blockchain developers and researchers with an authoritative guide to the Polymarket API, enabling them to integrate Polymarket data into their applications or analyses with confidence. Polymarket operates on the Polygon (Ethereum) blockchain, using smart contracts to create and manage prediction markets[2]. Each market is defined by a question (e.g., \u201cWill X happen by date Y?\u201d) and has a set of outcomes (for binary markets, typically \u201cYes\u201d and \u201cNo\u201d).\n\nPolymarket\u2019s API has evolved over time to its current \u201cGamma\u201d version. In earlier iterations of the platform, market data might have been accessed through different or more limited interfaces (including direct subgraph queries or ad-hoc endpoints). The Gamma API, introduced as a dedicated market data service, indexes all relevant on-chain and off-chain data and presents it in a developer-friendly REST format[14]. The term \u201cGamma\u201d in Polymarket\u2019s documentation refers to this hosted service that provides enriched market metadata on top of the raw on-chain data, such as human-readable event information, categorized listings, and aggregated statistics[14]. By naming it Gamma, Polymarket indicates a mature third iteration of its market data API (following presumably earlier alpha/beta phases), though the documentation primarily uses \u201cGamma\u201d to distinguish the market metadata API from other components.",

        "text": "Polymarket allows for the one way (for capital efficiency) conversion from No tokens to a collection of Yes tokens and USDC before resolution through a smart contract. get one or more order books, best price, spread, midpoint, last trade price ...\n\nUnified Polymarket APIs with Pydantic data validation - Clob, Gamma, Data, Web3, Websockets, GraphQL clients. ... Unified Polymarket APIs with Pydantic data validation - Clob, Gamma, Data, Web3, Websockets, GraphQL clients.\n\nThe different APIs represent Events/Markets differently (e.g. Event, QueryEvent / ClobMarket, GammaMarket, RewardsMarket) but they all use to the same underlying identifiers. Tokens are the blockchain implementation of Outcomes - tradable digital assets on the Polygon blockchain that users buy, hold and sell on Polygon. This helps ensure the logic of binary outcome prediction markets through smart contracts (e.g. collateralization, token prices going to $1.00 or $0.00 after resolution, splits/merges). Holding 1 Yes share + 1 No share in a Market (e.g. 'will-1-fed-rate-cut-happen-in-2025') covers the entire universe of possibilities and guarantees a $1.00 payout regardless of outcome. This mathematical relationship enables Polymarket's core mechanisms: splitting (1 USDC \u2192 1 Yes + 1 No) and merging (1 Yes + 1 No \u2192 1 USDC) at any point before resolution.\n\nSplits are the only way tokens are created. Either a user splits USDC into equal shares of the complementary tokens or Polymarket automatically splits USDC when it matches an Yes buy order at e.g. 30\u00a2 with a No buy order at 70\u00a2. Polymarket uses traditional exchange mechanics - a Central Limit Order Book (CLOB), where users place buy and sell orders that get matched by price and time priority. However, because the Yes and No outcomes form a complete probability universe, certain orders become mathematically equivalent - allowing the matching engine to find trades as exemplified above. This unified structure means every BUY order for Outcome 1 at price X is simultaneously visible as a SELL order for Outcome 2 at price (100\u00a2 - X), creating deeper liquidity and tighter spreads than separate order books would allow. If the Markets in and Event collectively cover a complete universe of possibilities (e.g.\n\nPolymarket allows for the one way (for capital efficiency) conversion from No tokens to a collection of Yes tokens and USDC before resolution through a smart contract. get one or more order books, best price, spread, midpoint, last trade price by token_id(s) ... get all active markets that offer rewards sorted by different metrics and ordered, filtered by a query, show your favourites from the web app - get_reward_markets() (naming would do with some work) ... get GammaMarkets with pagination (offset and limit), filter by slugs, market_ids, token_ids, condition_ids, tag_id or filtered by active, closed, archived, liquidity window, volume window, start date window, end date window and ordered ... get Events with pagination, filter by slugs, event_ids, tag_id or filtered by active, closed, archived, liquidity window, volume window, start date window, end date window and ordered ...",

        "text": "All historical trades can be fetched via the Polymarket CLOB REST API. A trade is initiated by a &quot;taker&quot; who creates a marketable limit order. This limit order can be matched against one or more resting limit orders on the associated book. A trade can be in various states as described below.\n\nBoth min_incentive_size and max_incentive_spread can be fetched alongside full market objects cia both the CLOB API and Markets API. Reward allocations for an epoch can be fetched via the Markets API. ... All outcomes on Polymarket are tokenized on the Polygon network. Specifically, Polymarket outcome shares are binary outcomes (ie \u201cYES\u201d and \u201cNO\u201d) represented using Gnosis\u2019 Conditional Token Framework (CTF). They are distinct ERC1155 tokens related to a parent condition and backed by some collateral. More technically, the binary outcome tokens are referred to as \u201cpositionIds\u201d in Gnosis\u2019s documentation. \u201cPositionIds\u201d are derived from a collateral token and distinct \u201ccollectionIds\u201d. \u201cCollectionIds\u201d are derived from a \u201cparentCollectionId\u201d, (always bytes32(0) in our case) a \u201cconditionId\u201d, and a unique \u201cindexSet\u201d. The \u201cindexSet\u201d is a 256 bit array denoting which outcome slots are in an outcome collection; it must be a nonempty proper subset of a condition\u2019s outcome slots.\n\nAll historical trades can be fetched via the Polymarket CLOB REST API. A trade is initiated by a \"taker\" who creates a marketable limit order. This limit order can be matched against one or more resting limit orders on the associated book. A trade can be in various states as described below. Note in some cases (due to gas limitations) the execution of a \"trade\" must be broken into multiple transactions in which case separate trade entities will be returned. To make these trade entires associable, there is a bucket_index field, a market_order field and a match_time field. Trades that have been broken into multiple trade objects can be reconciled by combining trade objects with the same market_order, match_time and incrementing bucket_indexs into a top level \"trade\" client side. This endpoint required a L2 Header. Get trades for the authenticated user based on the provided filters.\n\nThe CLOB provides detailed price history data for each traded token. ... The query parameters startTs/endTs are mutually exclusive to interval. The options for interval are: ... All market data necessary for market resolution is available on-chain (ie ancillaryData in UMA OO request) but Polymarket also provides a hosted service, Gamma, that indexes this data and provides additional market metadata (ie categorization, indexed volume, etc). This service is made available through a REST API. For public users, this resource is read only and can be used to fetch useful information about markets for things like non-profit research projects, alternative trading interfaces, automated trading systems etc. ... Gamma provides some organizational models. These include events, and markets. The most fundamental element is always markets and the other models simply provide additional organization.\n\nUnderlying all markets, and providing for an alternative trading mechanism to the central limit order book (CLOB) are fixed product market makers (FPMMs). These FPMMs are deployed upon market creation using a factory contract. As such, each market has a unique FPMM deployment/address. The addresses and associations of these deployments are indexed in the subgraph and made available via the Gamma API. The contracts themselves are also self-descriptive. As the name suggests, FPMMs implement a fixed (ie \"constant\") product scoring rule wherein the product of the tokens in the pool (ie the liquidity) is held constant. By maintaining this invariant, the price of a trade is calculated. Importantly, the tokens in the pool are outcome shares. Anyone can provide liquidity to the contract, and in return get ERC20 tokens representing their share of the liquidity pool.",

The database is initialized by src/rarb/data/database.py and stored at ~/.rarb/rarb.db.\n\nrarb is an automated trading bot that exploits price inefficiencies in Polymarket, a decentralized prediction market platform. The bot monitors up to 1,500 binary outcome markets in real-time via WebSocket connections, detects arbitrage opportunities using price analysis, and executes trades through Polymarket's Central Limit Order Book (CLOB) API. The project is structured as a Python package with a command-line interface (rarb command) and a web-based dashboard for monitoring. The codebase is organized into modular components for scanning, analysis, execution, and data management. Sources: pyproject.toml1-68 README.md1-139 src/rarb/__init__.py1-4 \u00b7 Polymarket markets have binary outcomes represented by YES and NO tokens. Upon market resolution, exactly one token pays out $1.00 while the other becomes worthless. This creates a mathematical certainty: purchasing both tokens guarantees a $1.00 payout regardless of outcome.\n\nWhen this condition occurs, the bot can purchase both tokens at a combined cost below the guaranteed $1.00 payout, locking in risk-free profit.         \"order_book\": order_book\n            }\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error fetching market data for {token_id}: {e}\")\n            return {}\n    \n    def place_market_order(\n        self, \n        token_id: str, \n        amount: float, \n        side: str,\n        order_type: OrderType = OrderType.FOK\n    ) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Place a market order\n        \n        Args:\n            token_id: The token ID to trade\n            amount: Amount in USDC\n            side: BUY or SELL\n            order_type: FOK (Fill or check_arbitrage_opportunity(self, yes_token_id: str, no_token_id: str) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Check for arbitrage opportunities between YES and NO tokens\n        Since YES + NO = $1.00 at settlement, if we can buy both for < $1.00, it's arbitrage\n        \n        Args:\n            yes_token_id: YES token ID\n            no_token_id: NO token ID\n            \n        Returns:\n            Arbitrage data if opportunity exists, None otherwise\n        \"\"\"\n        try:\n            yes_price = self.client.get_price(yes_token_id, side=\"BUY\")\n            no_price = self.client.get_price(no_token_id, side=\"BUY\")\n            \n            if yes_price and no_price:\n                combined_cost = yes_price + no_price\n                profit = 1.00 - combined_cost\n                profit_pct = (profit / combined_cost) * 100 if combined_cost > 0 else 0\n                \n                if profit > 0:\n                    logger.info(f\"Arbitrage opportunity found! Profit: ${profit:.4f} ({profit_pct:.2f}%)\")\n                    return {\n                        \"yes_token\": yes_token_id,\n                        \"no_token\": no_token_id,\n                        \"yes_price\": yes_price,\n                        \"no_price\": no_price,\n                        \"combined_cost\": combined_cost,\n                        \"profit\": profit,\n                        \"profit_pct\": profit_pct\n                    }\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error checking arbitrage: {e}\")\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def execute_arbitrage(self, arb_data: Dict, amount: float) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Execute an arbitrage trade\n        \n        Args:\n            arb_data: Arbitrage opportunity data\n            amount: Amount in USDC to invest\n            \n        Returns:\n            True if successful, False otherwise\n        \"\"\"\n        try:\n            # Calculate how much to buy of each token\n            yes_amount = amount * (arb_data[\"yes_price\"] / arb_data[\"combined_cost\"])\n            no_amount = amount * (arb_data[\"no_price\"] / arb_data[\"combined_cost\"])\n            \n            # Place both orders\n            yes_order = self.place_market_order(arb_data[\"yes_token\"], yes_amount, BUY)\n            no_order = self.place_market_order(arb_data[\"no_token\"], no_amount, BUY)\n            \n            if yes_order and no_order:\n                logger.info(f\"Arbitrage executed successfully! Expected profit: ${arb_data['profit'] * amount:.2f}\")\n                return True\n            else:\n                logger.error(\"Failed to execute complete arbitrage - one or both orders failed\")\n                return False\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error executing arbitrage: {e}\")\n            return False\n    \n    def simple_momentum_strategy(self, token_id: str, lookback_trades: int = 10) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Simple momentum strategy based on recent trades\n        \n        Args:\n            token_id: Token to analyze\n            lookback_trades: Number of recent trades to analyze\n            \n        Returns:\n            \"BUY\", \"SELL\", or None\n        \"\"\"\n        try:\n            # Get recent trades\n            trades = self.client.get_trades()\n            \n            if len(trades) < lookback_trades:\n                return None\n            \n            recent_trades = trades[:lookback_trades]\n            \n            # Calculate price momentum\n            prices = [float(trade.get('price', 0)) for trade in recent_trades]\n            avg_price = sum(prices) / len(prices)\n            current_price = self.client.get_last_trade_price(token_id)\n            \n            if current_price > avg_price * 1.02:  # 2% above average\n                return SELL\n            elif current_price < avg_price * 0.98:  # 2% below average\n                return BUY\n            \n            return None\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Error in momentum strategy: {e}\")\n            return None\n    \n    def get_balance(self) -> float:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get current USDC balance (simplified)\n        Note: This requires additional implementation based on your wallet type\n        \"\"\"\n        # This is a placeholder - actual implementation depends on wallet integration\n        logger.warning(\"Balance checking not fully implemented\")\n        return 0.0\n    \n    def run_monitoring_loop(self, token_ids: List[str], interval: int = 60):\n        \"\"\"\n        Run a continuous monitoring loop\n        \n        Args:\n            token_ids: List of token IDs to monitor\n            interval: Seconds between checks\n        \"\"\"\n        logger.info(f\"Starting monitoring loop for {len(token_ids)} tokens\")\n        \n        while True:\n            try:\n                for token_id in token_ids:\n                    market_data = self.get_market_data(token_id)\n                    logger.info(f\"Token {token_id}: Mid={market_data.get('midpoint')}, Spread={market_data.get('spread')}\")\n                \n                time.sleep(interval)\n            except KeyboardInterrupt:\n                logger.info(\"Monitoring loop stopped by user\")\n                break\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f\"Error in monitoring loop: {e}\")\n                time.sleep(interval)\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"\n    Main entry point for the bot\n    \"\"\"\n    # Clone or download this repository\n\n2. Install dependencies:\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n3. Set up your environment variables:\n```bash\ncp .env.example .env\n# Edit .env with your credentials\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Getting Your Private Key\n\n**For MetaMask/EOA wallets:**\n1. Open MetaMask\n2. Click the three dots \u2192 Account Details \u2192 Export Private Key\n3. Enter your password and copy the key\n4. Set `POLYMARKET_SIGNATURE_TYPE=0`\n\n**For Magic/Email wallets:**\n1. You'll need to extract your key from the Magic SDK\n2. Set `POLYMARKET_SIGNATURE_TYPE=1`\n3. Set your `POLYMARKET_FUNDER` address\n\n### Setting Token Allowances\n\nIf using an EOA wallet (MetaMask), you must set token allowances before trading:\n\n```python\nfrom py_clob_client.client import ClobClient\nfrom py_clob_client.exceptions import PolyApiException\n\nclient = ClobClient(\n    \"https://clob.polymarket.com\",\n    key=YOUR_PRIVATE_KEY,\n    chain_id=137\n)\n\n# Set allowances\ntry:\n    client.set_token_allowance(token_id, amount)\n    print(\"Allowances set successfully\")\nexcept PolyApiException as e:\n    print(f\"Error: {e}\")\n```\n\n## Getting Token IDs\n\nYou need token IDs to trade specific markets. Get them from the Gamma API:\n\n```python\nimport requests\n\n# Get all active markets\nresponse = requests.get(\"https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/markets\")\nmarkets = response.json()\n\nfor market in markets[:5]:  # Show first 5\n    print(f\"Market: {market['question']}\")\n    print(f\"YES Token: {market['tokens'][0]['token_id']}\")\n    print(f\"NO Token: {market['tokens'][1]['token_id']}\")\n    print()\n```\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Market Monitoring\n\n```python\nfrom polymarket_bot import PolymarketBot\n\n# Initialize bot\nbot = PolymarketBot(\n    private_key=\"your_private_key\",\n    signature_type=0  # EOA wallet\n)\n\n# Get market data\ntoken_id = \"your_token_id_here\"\ndata = bot.get_market_data(token_id)\nprint(f\"Current price: ${data['midpoint']}\")\nprint(f\"Spread: ${data['spread']}\")\n```\n\n### Arbitrage Detection\n\n```python\n# Check for arbitrage between YES and NO tokens\nyes_token = \"yes_token_id\"\nno_token = \"no_token_id\"\n\narb = bot.check_arbitrage_opportunity(yes_token, no_token)\nif arb:\n    print(f\"Arbitrage found! Profit: ${arb['profit']:.4f}\")\n    \n    # Execute the trade\n    success = bot.execute_arbitrage(arb, amount=10.0)\n    if success:\n        print(\"Arbitrage executed successfully!\")\n```\n\n### Placing Orders\n\n```python\nfrom py_clob_client.order_builder.constants import BUY, SELL\nfrom py_clob_client.clob_types import OrderType\n\n# Place a market order\nbot.place_market_order(\n    token_id=\"your_token_id\",\n    amount=10.0,  # USDC\n    side=BUY,\n    order_type=OrderType.FOK  # Fill or Kill\n)\n```\n\n### Running Continuous Monitoring\n\n```python\n# Monitor multiple markets\ntoken_ids = [\n    \"token_id_1\",\n    \"token_id_2\",\n    \"token_id_3\"\n]\n\n# Run monitoring loop (checks every 30 seconds)\nbot.run_monitoring_loop(token_ids, interval=30)\n```\n\n## Trading Strategies\n\n### 1. Arbitrage Strategy\n\nThe bot can detect when YES + NO token prices sum to less than $1.00, creating a risk-free arbitrage opportunity:\n\n```\nMarket: \"Will BTC exceed $100k by Dec 31?\"\nYES token @ $0.48\nNO token @ $0.49\nCombined: $0.97\nGuaranteed payout: $1.00\nRisk-free profit: $0.03 (3.09% return)\n```\n\n### 2. Momentum Strategy\n\nTrade based on recent price movements:\n- Buy when price is 2% below recent average\n- Sell when price is 2% above recent average\n\n### 3. Custom Strategy Template\n\n```python\ndef custom_strategy(self, token_id: str) -> Optional[str]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implement your own trading logic here\n    \n    Returns:\n        \"BUY\", \"SELL\", or None\n    \"\"\"\n    market_data = self.get_market_data(token_id)\n    \n    # Your logic here\n    if some_buy_condition:\n        return BUY\n    elif some_sell_condition:\n        return SELL\n    \n    return None\n```\n\n## Risk Management\n\n**Important considerations:**\n\n1. **Start Small**: Test with small amounts first\n2. **Set Position Limits**: Never risk more than you can afford to lose\n3. **Monitor Liquidity**: Ensure markets have enough liquidity for your trades\n4. **Gas Fees**: Consider Polygon gas fees in your profit calculations\n5. **Slippage**: Market orders may execute at different prices than expected\n\n## API Rate Limits\n\nFrom the documentation:\n- Free tier: ~100 requests per minute\n- Higher volume users: Consider premium tiers\n\n## Common Issues\n\n### \"Not enough balance/allowance\" error\n- Ensure your wallet has USDC.e on Polygon\n- Set token allowances (for EOA wallets)\n\n### Orders not executing\n- Check that the market has sufficient liquidity\n- Verify your order size meets minimum requirements\n- Ensure your wallet is funded\n\n### Slow performance\n- Order signing can take ~1 second\n- Use async operations for better performance\n- Consider running on a VPS for 24/7 operation\n\n## Advanced Features\n\n### WebSocket Integration\n\nFor real-time updates, consider using WebSockets:\n\n```python\n# Example using websockets library\nimport websocket\nimport json\n\ndef on_message(ws, message):\n    data = json.loads(message)\n    print(f\"Update: {data}\")\n\nws = websocket.WebSocketApp(\n    \"wss://clob-ws.polymarket.com\",\n    on_message=on_message\n)\nws.run_forever()\n```\n\n### Backtesting\n\nTest strategies on historical data before live trading:\n\n```python\nfrom py_clob_client.client import ClobClient\n\nclient = ClobClient(\"https://clob.polymarket.com\")\n\n# Get historical price data\nhistory = client.get_price_history(\n    token_id=\"your_token_id\",\n    interval=\"1h\",\n    startTs=start_timestamp,\n    endTs=end_timestamp\n)\n\n# Backtest your strategy on historical data\n```\n\n## Resources\n\n- [Polymarket       "file_text": "\"\"\"\nUtility script to discover active Polymarket markets and get token IDs\n\"\"\"\n\nimport requests\nfrom typing import List, Dict\nimport json\n\n\ndef get_active_markets(limit: int = 20) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Fetch active markets from Polymarket Gamma API\n    \n    Args:\n        limit: Number of markets to fetch\n        \n    Returns:\n        List of market data\n    \"\"\"\n    url = \"https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/markets\"\n    params = {\n        \"limit\": limit,\n        \"active\": \"true\"\n    }\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(url, params=params)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:\n        print(f\"Error fetching markets: {e}\")\n        return []\n\n\ndef get_market_by_slug(slug: str) -> Dict:\n    \"\"\"\n    Get a specific market by its slug\n    \n    Args:\n        slug: Market slug (from URL)\n        \n    Returns:\n        Market data\n    \"\"\"\n    url = f\"https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/markets/{slug}\"\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(url)\n        response.raise_for_status()\n        return response.json()\n    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:\n        print(f\"Error fetching market: {e}\")\n        return {}\n\n\ndef display_markets(markets: List[Dict], detailed: bool = False):\n    \"\"\"\n    Display market information in a readable format\n    \n    Args:\n        markets: List of market data\n        detailed: Show detailed information\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"\\n{'='*80}\")\n    print(f\"Found {len(markets)} Active Markets\")\n    print(f\"{'='*80}\\n\")\n    \n    for i, market in enumerate(markets, 1):\n        print(f\"{i}. {market.get('question', 'N/A')}\")\n        print(f\"   Description: {market.get('description', 'N/A')[:100]}...\")\n        print(f\"   Category: {market.get('category', 'N/A')}\")\n        print(f\"   Volume: ${market.get('volume', 0):,.2f}\")\n        print(f\"   Liquidity: ${market.get('liquidity', 0):,.2f}\")\n        \n        # Token information\n        tokens = market.get('tokens', [])\n        if tokens:\n            print(f\"   Tokens:\")\n            for token in tokens:\n                outcome = token.get('outcome', 'N/A')\n                token_id = Install Python 3.9+ if you don't have it:\n   https://www.python.org/downloads/\n\n2. Open terminal/command prompt\n\n3. Create a project folder:\n\"\"\"\n\n# On Mac/Linux:\nmkdir ~/polymarket-bot\ncd ~/polymarket-bot\n\n# On Windows:\nmkdir C:\\polymarket-bot\ncd C:\\polymarket-bot\n\n\"\"\"\n4. Copy all the bot files to this folder:\n   - polymarket_bot.py\n   - discover_markets.py\n   - requirements.txt\n   - .env.example\n   - README.md\n\n5. Install dependencies:\n\"\"\"\n\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# If you get errors, try:\npip install py-clob-client web3==6.14.0 python-dotenv requests --upgrade\n\n\"\"\"\n6. Create your .env file:\n\"\"\"\n\n# Copy the example\ncp .env.example .env\n\n# Edit .env with your favorite text editor\n# On Mac: open .env\n# On Windows: notepad .env\n\n\"\"\"\nFill in:\nPOLYMARKET_PRIVATE_KEY=your_private_key_without_0x_prefix\nPOLYMARKET_SIGNATURE_TYPE=0\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# STEP 3: SET TOKEN ALLOWANCES (2 minutes) - CRITICAL!\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\nIf using MetaMask/EOA wallet, you MUST do this before trading!\nThis gives Polymarket permission to move your USDC.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom py_clob_client.client import ClobClient\nfrom py_clob_client.constants import COLLATERAL_TOKEN_ADDRESS\nimport os\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\n\nload_dotenv()\n\n# Your private key from .env\nprivate_key = os.getenv(\"POLYMARKET_PRIVATE_KEY\")\n\nclient = ClobClient(\n    host=\"https://clob.polymarket.com\",\n    key=private_key,\n    chain_id=137,\n    signature_type=0  # EOA\n)\n\nprint(\"Setting allowances... this will cost a small gas fee\")\n\n# Set USDC allowance\nclient.set_token_allowance(\n    token_address=COLLATERAL_TOKEN_ADDRESS,\n    amount=1000000  # Allow up to 1M USDC\n)\n\nprint(\"\u2713 Allowances set! You're ready to trade.\")\n\n\"\"\"\nSave this as setup_allowances.py and run:\npython setup_allowances.py\n\nYou only need to do this ONCE per wallet.\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# STEP 4: FIND PROFITABLE MARKETS (3 minutes)\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\nNow let's find markets to trade!\n\"\"\"\n\n# Run the market discovery script:\npython discover_markets.py\n\n\"\"\"\nThis will show you:\n- Active markets\n- Token IDs you need for trading\n- Current prices\n- Trading volume\n\nLook for markets with:\n\u2713 High volume (> $10,000)\n\u2713 Good liquidity\n\u2713 Topics you understand\n\nThe script outputs token_ids.json - use these in your bot!\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# STEP 5: TEST WITH A SMALL TRADE (2 minutes)\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\nLet's test with a manual trade first\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom polymarket_bot import PolymarketBot\nfrom py_clob_client.order_builder.constants import BUY\nimport os\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\n\nload_dotenv()\n\n# Initialize bot\nbot = PolymarketBot(\n    private_key=os.getenv(\"POLYMARKET_PRIVATE_KEY\"),\n    signature_type=0\n)\n\n# Get a token ID from discover_markets.py output\n# Example: \"71321045679252212594626385532706912750332728571942532289631379312455583992833\"\ntest_token_id = \"YOUR_TOKEN_ID_HERE\"\n\n# Check current price\ndata = bot.get_market_data(test_token_id)\nprint(f\"Current price: ${data['midpoint']:.4f}\")\nprint(f\"Spread: ${data['spread']:.4f}\")\n\n# Place a SMALL test order ($5)\nprint(\"\\nPlacing test order...\")\nresponse = bot.place_market_order(\n    token_id=test_token_id,\n    amount=5.0,  # $5 USDC - start small!\n    side=BUY\n)\n\nprint(f\"Order response: {response}\")\n\n\"\"\"\nIf this works, you're ready for automated trading!\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# STEP 6: RUN ARBITRAGE BOT (MONEY-MAKING TIME!)\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\nThe arbitrage strategy is the safest way to make money.\nIt finds risk-free opportunities where YES + NO < $1.00\n\nCreate a file called run_arbitrage.py:\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom polymarket_bot import PolymarketBot\nfrom py_clob_client.order_builder.constants import BUY\nimport os\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\nimport time\nimport json\n\nload_dotenv()\n\n# Initialize bot\nbot = PolymarketBot(\n    private_key=os.getenv(\"POLYMARKET_PRIVATE_KEY\"),\n    signature_type=0\n)\n\n# Load token IDs from discover_markets.py\nwith open('token_ids.json', 'r') as f:\n    markets = json.load(f)\n\n# Configuration\nMIN_PROFIT_PCT = 1.0  # Minimum 1% profit\nTRADE_AMOUNT = 10.0   # $10 per trade - adjust based on your capital\nCHECK_INTERVAL = 30   # Seconds between checks\n\nprint(\"Starting Arbitrage Bot...\")\nprint(f\"Minimum profit: {MIN_PROFIT_PCT}%\")\nprint(f\"Trade amount: ${TRADE_AMOUNT}\")\nprint(\"=\"*60)\n\ntrades_executed = 0\ntotal_profit = 0.0\n\nwhile True:\n    try:\n        # Check each market for arbitrage\n        for market in markets:\n            tokens = market['tokens']\n            \n            if len(tokens) < 2:\n                continue\n            \n            yes_token = tokens[0]['token_id']\n            no_token = tokens[1]['token_id']\n            \n            # Check for arbitrage\n            arb = bot.check_arbitrage_opportunity(yes_token, no_token)\n            \n            if arb and arb['profit_pct'] >= MIN_PROFIT_PCT:\n                print(f\"\\n\ud83c\udfaf ARBITRAGE FOUND!\")\n                print(f\"Market: {market['question']}\")\n                print(f\"YES price: ${arb['yes_price']:.4f}\")\n                print(f\"NO price: ${arb['no_price']:.4f}\")\n                print(f\"Combined: ${arb['combined_cost']:.4f}\")\n                print(f\"Profit: ${arb['profit']:.4f} ({arb['profit_pct']:.2f}%)\")\n                \n                # Execute the trade\n                print(f\"\\nExecuting ${TRADE_AMOUNT} arbitrage trade...\")\n                success = bot.execute_arbitrage(arb, TRADE_AMOUNT)\n                \n                if success:\n                    trades_executed += 1\n                    expected_profit = arb['profit'] * TRADE_AMOUNT\n                    total_profit += expected_profit\n                    \n                    print(f\"\u2713 Trade #{trades_executed} executed!\")\n                    print(f\"Expected profit: ${expected_profit:.2f}\")\n                    print(f\"Total profit: ${total_profit:.2f}\")\n                else:\n                    print(f\"\u2717 Trade failed - continuing...\")\n        \n        # Wait before next check\n        print(f\"\\nChecked {len(markets)} markets. Waiting {CHECK_INTERVAL}s...\")\n        print(f\"Stats: {trades_executed} trades, ${total_profit:.2f} total profit\")\n        time.sleep(CHECK_INTERVAL)\n        \n    except KeyboardInterrupt:\n        print(\"\\n\\nBot stopped by user\")\n        print(f\"Final stats: {trades_executed} trades, ${total_profit:.2f} profit\")\n        break\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error: {e}\")\n        time.sleep(CHECK_INTERVAL)\n\n\"\"\"\nRun it:\npython run_arbitrage.py\n\nLet it run 24/7 to catch opportunities!\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# STEP 7: SCALE UP (After you're profitable)\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\nOnce you're making money consistently:\n\n1. INCREASE CAPITAL\n   - Start with $50-100\n   - After 1 week of profit, move to $500-1000\n   - Scale slowly based on results\n\n2. RUN ON A SERVER (24/7 operation)\n   - Use a VPS like DigitalOcean ($5/month) or AWS\n   - Install the bot on the server\n   - Run in background: nohup python run_arbitrage.py &\n   - Or use screen/tmux to keep it running\n\n3. OPTIMIZE SETTINGS\n   - Lower MIN_PROFIT_PCT if you're missing trades (try 0.5%)\n   - Increase CHECK_INTERVAL if hitting rate limits\n   - Adjust TRADE_AMOUNT based on market liquidity\n\n4. MONITOR PERFORMANCE\n   - Keep logs of all trades\n   - Calculate actual ROI\n   - Adjust strategy based on data\n\n5. ADD MORE STRATEGIES\n   - Momentum trading\n   - Market making\n   - News-based trading\n   - Multi-market arbitrage\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# EXPECTED RETURNS\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\nREALISTIC EXPECTATIONS:\n\nArbitrage Strategy (Conservative):\n- Opportunities: 5-20 per day\n- Profit per trade: 0.5% - 3%\n- With $100 capital: $1-5 per day\n- With $1000 capital: $10-50 per day\n- Annual return: 20-50% (if consistent)\n\nRisk Level: LOW (arbitrage is risk-free if executed properly)\n\nIMPORTANT: \n- Past performance doesn't guarantee future results\n- Market conditions change\n- Competition from other bots reduces opportunities\n- Gas fees eat into small profits\n- Slippage can reduce profits\n\nSTART SMALL, LEARN, THEN SCALE!\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# TROUBLESHOOTING\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\nProblem: \"Not enough balance/allowance\"\nSolution: \n- Check you have USDC on Polygon (not Ethereum!)\n- Run setup_allowances.py again\n- Verify with: client.get_allowances()\n\nProblem: \"Orders not filling\"\nSolution:\n- Market may have low liquidity\n- Your price may be too far from market\n- Try smaller order sizes\n\nProblem: \"Rate limit exceeded\"\nSolution:\n- Increase CHECK_INTERVAL\n- Reduce number of markets monitored\n- Consider premium API tier\n\nProblem: \"Bot not finding arbitrage\"\nSolution:\n- Markets are efficient, opportunities are rare\n- Lower MIN_PROFIT_PCT threshold\n- Monitor more markets\n- Be patient - opportunities come in bursts\n\nProblem: Bot crashes\nSolution:\n- Check error logs\n- Ensure stable internet connection\n- Add more error handling\n- Run on a server instead of laptop\n\"\"\"\n\n# ============================================================================\n# SAFETY TIPS\n# ============================================================================\n\n\"\"\"\n\ud83d\udd12 SECURITY:\n- NEVER share your private key\n- Use a separate wallet for bot trading\n- Don't commit .env to GitHub\n- Keep backup of private key in safe place\n\n\ud83d\udcb0 RISK MANAGEMENT:\n- Start with small amounts ($50-100)\n- Never invest more than you can afford to lose\n- Set position limits (max per trade)\n- Monitor bot daily at first\n- Take profits regularly\n\n\u2696\ufe0f LEGAL:\n- Check if prediction markets are legal in your jurisdiction\n- Keep records for taxes\n- Understand you're trading real money\n- Read Polymarket terms of service\n\n\ud83c\udfaf STRATEGY:\n- Focus on arbitrage first (lowest risk)\n- Don't get greedy - Press Ctrl+C to stop\\n\")\n    \n    # Main loop\n    iteration = 0\n    while True:\n        try:\n            iteration += 1\n            logger.info(f\"--- Iteration {iteration} ---\")\n            \n            # Main loop\n    while bot_running:\n        try:\n            update_runtime()\n            \n            # Check each market for arbitrage\n            for market in valid_markets:\n                if not bot_running:\n                    break\n                \n                try:\n                    tokens = market['tokens']\n                    yes_token = tokens[0]['token_id']\n                    no_token = tokens[1]['token_id']\n                    \n                    # Check for arbitrage\n                    arb = bot_instance.check_arbitrage_opportunity(yes_token, no_token)\n                    \n                    if arb and arb['profit_pct'] >= bot_state['config']['min_profit']:\n                        bot_state['stats']['opportunities_found'] += 1\n                        \n                        # Add to current opportunities\n                        opportunity = {\n                            'id': str(time.time()),\n                            'market': market.get('question', 'Unknown Market'),\n                            'yes_token': yes_token,\n                            'no_token': no_token,\n                            'yes_price': arb['yes_price'],\n                            'no_price': arb['no_price'],\n                            'profit': arb['profit'],\n                            'profit_pct': arb['profit_pct'],\n                            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()\n                        }\n                        \n                        bot_state['current_opportunities'].insert(0, opportunity)\n                        bot_state['current_opportunities'] = bot_state['current_opportunities'][:10]\n                        \n                        add_log(\n                            f\"Arbitrage found: {arb['profit_pct']:.2f}% profit on {market.get('question', 'Unknown')[:50]}\",\n                            'success'\n                        )\n                        \n                        # Broadcast opportunity to frontend\n                        socketio.emit('opportunity', opportunity)\n                        \n                        # Auto-execute if enabled (you can add this as a config option)\n                        auto_execute = os.getenv('AUTO_EXECUTE', 'true').lower() == 'true'\n                        \n                        if auto_execute:\n                            add_log(f\"Executing trade for ${bot_state['config']['trade_amount']}\", 'info')\n                            \n                            success = bot_instance.execute_arbitrage(\n                                arb, \n                                bot_state['config']['trade_amount']\n                            )\n                            \n                            if success:\n                                expected_profit = arb['profit'] * bot_state['config']['trade_amount']\n                                bot_state['stats']['trades_executed'] += 1\n                                bot_state['stats']['total_profit'] += expected_profit\n                                \n                                # Add to recent trades\n                                trade = {\n                                    'id': str(time.time()),\n                                    'market': market.get('question', 'Unknown'),\n                                    'profit': expected_profit,\n                                    'profit_pct': arb['profit_pct'],\n                                    'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()\n                                }\n                                bot_state['recent_trades'].insert(0, trade)\n                                bot_state['recent_trades'] = bot_state['recent_trades'][:20]\n                                \n                                add_log(f\"Trade executed! Profit: ${expected_profit:.2f}\", 'success')\n                                socketio.emit('trade', trade)\n                            else:\n                                bot_state['stats']['failed_trades'] += 1\n                                add_log('Trade execution failed', 'error')\n                \n                except Exception as e:\n                    add_log(f'Error checking market: {str(e)}', 'error')\n                    continue\n            \n            # Broadcast stats update\n            socketio.emit('stats', bot_state['stats'])\n            \n            # Wait before next iteration\n            add_log(f'Scan complete. Start bot in background thread\n    bot_thread = threading.Thread(target=bot_loop, daemon=True)\n    bot_thread.start()\n    \n    add_log('Bot started', 'success')\n    \n    return jsonify({'message': 'Bot started successfully'})\n\n\n@app.route('/api/stop', methods=['POST'])\ndef stop_bot():\n    \"\"\"Stop the trading bot\"\"\"\n    global bot_running\n    \n    if bot_state['status'] != 'running':\n        return jsonify({'error': 'Bot is not running'}), 400\n    \n    bot_running = False\n    bot_state['status'] = 'stopped'\n    \n    add_log('Stopping bot...', 'warning')\n    \n    return jsonify({'message': 'Bot stopped'})\n\n\n@app.route('/api/config', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef handle_config():\n    \"\"\"Get or update bot configuration\"\"\"\n    if request.method == 'GET':\n        return jsonify(bot_state['config'])\n    \n    elif request.method == 'POST':\n        data = request.json\n        \n        # Update config\n        if 'min_profit' in data:\n            bot_state['config']['min_profit'] = float(data['min_profit'])\n        if 'trade_amount' in data:\n            bot_state['config']['trade_amount'] = float(data['trade_amount'])\n        if 'poll_interval' in data:\n            bot_state['config']['poll_interval'] = int(data['poll_interval'])\n        \n        add_log('Configuration updated', 'info')\n        \n        return jsonify({'message': 'Configuration updated', 'config': bot_state['config']})\n\n\n@app.route('/api/opportunities', methods=['GET'])\ndef get_opportunities():\n    \"\"\"Get current arbitrage opportunities\"\"\"\n    return jsonify(bot_state['current_opportunities'])\n\n\n@app.route('/api/trades', methods=['GET'])\ndef get_trades():\n    \"\"\"Get recent trades\"\"\"\n    return jsonify(bot_state['recent_trades'])\n\n\n@app.route('/api/logs', methods=['GET'])\ndef get_logs():\n    \"\"\"Get activity logs\"\"\"\n    return jsonify(bot_state['logs'])\n\n\n@app.route('/api/execute', methods=['POST'])\ndef execute_trade():\n    \"\"\"Manually execute a specific trade\"\"\"\n    data = request.json\n    \n    if not bot_instance:\n        return jsonify({'error': 'Bot not initialized'}), 400\n    \n    yes_token = data.get('yes_token')\n    no_token = data.get('no_token')\n    amount = data.get('amount', bot_state['config']['trade_amount'])\n    \n    try:\n        #   <script>\n        const API_URL = 'http://localhost:5000';\n        let socket;\n        let botStatus = 'stopped';\n        \n        // Initialize\n        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n            connectToServer();\n            loadStatus();\n        });\n        \n        // Connect to WebSocket\n        function connectToServer() {\n            socket = io(API_URL);\n            \n            socket.on('connect', () => {\n                updateAPIStatus(true);\n                addLog('Connected to server', 'success');\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('disconnect', () => {\n                updateAPIStatus(false);\n                addLog('Disconnected from server', 'error');\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('log', (data) => {\n                addLog(data.message, data.type);\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('stats', (data) => {\n                updateStats(data);\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('opportunity', (data) => {\n                addOpportunity(data);\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('trade', (data) => {\n                addTrade(data);\n            });\n        }\n        \n        // Update API status\n        function updateAPIStatus(connected) {\n            const statusEl = document.getElementById('api-status');\n            const statusTextEl = document.getElementById('api-status-text');\n            \n            if (connected) {\n                statusEl.className = 'text-green-500';\n                statusTextEl.textContent = 'Connected';\n            } else {\n                statusEl.className = 'text-red-500';\n                statusTextEl.textContent = 'Disconnected';\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Load current status\n        async function loadStatus() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/status`);\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                botStatus = data.status;\n                updateBotUI();\n                updateStats(data.stats);\n                \n                // Load config\n                document.getElementById('min-profit').value = data.config.min_profit;\n                document.getElementById('trade-amount').value = data.config.trade_amount;\n                document.getElementById('poll-interval').value = data.config.poll_interval;\n                \n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Failed to load status:', error);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Toggle bot\n        async function toggleBot() {\n            const endpoint = botStatus === 'running' ? '/api/stop' : '/api/start';\n            \n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}${endpoint}`, {\n                    method: 'POST'\n                });\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                botStatus = botStatus === 'running' ? 'stopped' : 'running';\n                updateBotUI();\n                \n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Failed to toggle bot:', error);\n                addLog('Failed to toggle bot: ' + error.message, 'error');\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Update bot UI\n        function updateBotUI() {\n            const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('bot-toggle');\n            const botIcon = document.getElementById('bot-icon');\n            const botText = document.getElementById('bot-text');\n            const statusBanner = document.getElementById('status-banner');\n            const statusDot = document.getElementById('status-dot');\n            const statusText = document.getElementById('status-text');\n            \n            if (botStatus === 'running') {\n                toggleBtn.className = 'px-6 py-2 rounded-lg font-semibold transition-all flex items-center gap-2 shadow-lg bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600 shadow-red-500/50';\n                botIcon.innerHTML = '<path stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\" stroke-width=\"2\" d=\"M10 9v6m4-6v6m7-3a9 9 0 11-18 0 9 9 0 0118 0z\"/>';\n                botText.textContent = 'Stop Bot';\n                statusDot.className = 'w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-green-500 animate-pulse';\n                statusText.textContent = 'Bot is actively scanning markets';\n            } else {\n                toggleBtn.className = 'px-6 py-2 rounded-lg font-semibold transition-all flex items-center gap-2 shadow-lg bg-gradient-to-r from-indigo-500 to-violet-500 hover:from-indigo-600 hover:to-violet-600 shadow-indigo-500/50';\n                botIcon.innerHTML = '<path stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\" stroke-width=\"2\" d=\"M14.752 11.168l-3.197-2.132A1 1 0 0010 9.87v4.263a1 1 0 001.555.832l3.197-2.132a1 1 0 000-1.664z\"/><path stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\" stroke-width=\"2\" d=\"M21 12a9 9 0 11-18 0 9 9 0 0118 0z\"/>';\n                botText.textContent = 'Start Bot';\n                statusDot.className = 'w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-amber-500';\n                statusText.textContent = 'Bot is stopped';\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Update stats\n        function updateStats(stats) {\n            document.getElementById('total-profit').textContent = stats.total_profit.toFixed(2);\n            document.getElementById('trades-executed').textContent = stats.trades_executed;\n            document.getElementById('opportunities-found').textContent = stats.opportunities_found;\n            document.getElementById('runtime').textContent = stats.runtime;\n            \n            const avgProfit = stats.trades_executed > 0 ? stats.total_profit / stats.trades_executed : 0;\n            document.getElementById('avg-profit').textContent = avgProfit.toFixed(2);\n        }\n        \n        // Add log entry\n        function addLog(message, type = 'info') {\n            const container = document.getElementById('log-container');\n            const now = new Date();\n            const time = now.toLocaleTimeString();\n            \n            const logEl = document.createElement('div');\n            logEl.className = 'text-xs p-2 rounded glass border-l-2 border-indigo-500 slide-up mono';\n            \n            let icon = '';\n            let colorClass = 'text-gray-300';\n            \n            if (type === 'success') {\n                icon = '<svg class=\"w-3 h-3 text-green-400\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\"><path stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\" stroke-width=\"2\" d=\"M5 13l4 4L19 7\"/></svg>';\n                colorClass = 'text-green-300';\n            } else if (type === 'error') {\n                icon = '<svg class=\"w-3 h-3 text-red-400\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\"><path stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\" stroke-width=\"2\" d=\"M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12\"/></svg>';\n                colorClass = 'text-red-300';\n            } else if (type === 'warning') {\n                icon = '<svg class=\"w-3 h-3 text-amber-400\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"currentColor\" viewBox=\"0 0 24 24\"><path stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\" stroke-width=\"2\" d=\"M12 9v2m0 4h.01m-6.938 4h13.856c1.54 0 2.502-1.667 1.732-3L13.732 4c-.77-1.333-2.694-1.333-3.464 0L3.34 16c-.77 1.333.192 3 1.732 3z\"/></svg>';\n                colorClass = 'text-amber-300';\n            }\n            \n            logEl.innerHTML = `\n                <div class=\"flex items-center gap-2 mb-1\">\n                    <span class=\"text-gray-500\">${time}</span>\n                    ${icon}\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"${colorClass}\">${message}</div>\n            `;\n            \n            container.insertBefore(logEl, container.firstChild);\n            \n            // Keep only last 50 logs\n            while (container.children.length > 50) {\n                container.removeChild(container.lastChild);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Add opportunity\n        function addOpportunity(opp) {\n            const container = document.getElementById('opportunities-list');\n            \n            // Clear empty state\n            if (container.querySelector('.text-center')) {\n                container.innerHTML = '';\n            }\n            \n            const oppEl = document.createElement('div');\n            oppEl.className = 'p-4 hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors slide-up';\n            oppEl.innerHTML = `\n                <div class=\"flex items-center justify-between mb-2\">\n                    <span class=\"font-medium text-sm\">${opp.market.substring(0, 50)}...</span>\n                    <span class=\"text-green-400 font-bold mono\">${parseFloat(opp.profit_pct).toFixed(2)}% profit</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class=\"grid grid-cols-3 gap-4 text-sm mono\">\n                    <div>\n                        <span class=\"text-gray-400 block\">YES Price</span>\n                        <span class=\"text-white\">$${parseFloat(opp.yes_price).toFixed(4)}</span>\n                    </div>\n                    <div>\n                        <span class=\"text-gray-400 block\">NO Price</span>\n                        <span class=\"text-white\">$${parseFloat(opp.no_price).toFixed(4)}</span>\n                    </div>\n                    <div>\n                        <span class=\"text-gray-400 block\">Profit</span>\n                        <span class=\"text-green-400\">$${parseFloat(opp.profit).toFixed(4)}</span>\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            `;\n            \n            container.insertBefore(oppEl, container.firstChild);\n            \n            // Update count\n            document.getElementById('opp-count').textContent = `${container.children.length} Active`;\n            \n            // Keep only last 10\n            while (container.children.length > 10) {\n                container.removeChild(container.lastChild);\n            }\n        }\n        \n   <script>\n        const API_URL = 'http://localhost:5000';\n        let socket;\n        let botStatus = 'stopped';\n        \n        // Initialize\n        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n            connectToServer();\n            loadStatus();\n        });\n        \n        // Connect to WebSocket\n        function connectToServer() {\n            socket = io(API_URL);\n            \n            socket.on('connect', () => {\n                updateAPIStatus(true);\n                addLog('Connected to server', 'success');\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('disconnect', () => {\n                updateAPIStatus(false);\n                addLog('Disconnected from server', 'error');\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('log', (data) => {\n                addLog(data.message, data.type);\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('stats', (data) => {\n                updateStats(data);\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('opportunity', (data) => {\n                addOpportunity(data);\n            });\n            \n            socket.on('trade', (data) => {\n                addTrade(data);\n            });\n        }\n        \n        // Update API status\n        function updateAPIStatus(connected) {\n            const statusEl = document.getElementById('api-status');\n            const statusTextEl = document.getElementById('api-status-text');\n            \n            if (connected) {\n                statusEl.className = 'text-green-500';\n                statusTextEl.textContent = 'Connected';\n            } else {\n                statusEl.className = 'text-red-500';\n                statusTextEl.textContent = 'Disconnected';\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Load current status\n        async function loadStatus() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}/api/status`);\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                botStatus = data.status;\n                updateBotUI();\n                updateStats(data.stats);\n                \n                // Load config\n                document.getElementById('min-profit').value = data.config.min_profit;\n                document.getElementById('trade-amount').value = data.config.trade_amount;\n                document.getElementById('poll-interval').value = data.config.poll_interval;\n                \n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Failed to load status:', error);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Toggle bot\n        async function toggleBot() {\n            const endpoint = botStatus === 'running' ? '/api/stop' : '/api/start';\n            \n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_URL}${endpoint}`, {\n                    method: 'POST'\n                });\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                botStatus = botStatus === 'running' ? 'stopped' : 'running';\n                updateBotUI();\n                \n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Failed to toggle bot:', error);\n                addLog('Failed to toggle bot: ' + error.message, 'error');\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Update bot UI\n        function updateBotUI() {\n            const toggleBtn = document.getElementById('bot-toggle');\n            const botIcon = document.getElementById('bot-icon');\n            const botText = document.getElementById('bot-text');\n            const statusBanner = document.getElementById('status-banner');\n            const statusDot = document.getElementById('status-dot');\n            const statusText = document.getElementById('status-text');\n            \n            if (botStatus === 'running') {\n                toggleBtn.className = 'px-6 py-2 rounded-lg font-semibold transition-all flex items-center gap-2 shadow-lg bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600 shadow-red-500/50';\n                botIcon.innerHTML = '<path stroke-linecap=\"round\" stroke-linejoin=\"round\" stroke-width=\"2\" d=\"M10 9v6m4-6v6m7-3a9 9 0 11-18 0 9 9 0 0118 document.getElementById('total-profit').textContent = stats.total_profit.toFixed(2);\n            document.getElementById('trades-executed').textContent = stats.trades_executed;\n            document.getElementById('opportunities-found').textContent = stats.opportunities_found;\n            document.getElementById('runtime').textContent = stats.runtime;\n            \n            const time = now.toLocaleTimeString();\n            \n            const logEl = document.createElement('div');\n            logEl.className = 'text-xs p-2 rounded glass border-l-2 border-indigo-500 slide-up mono';\n            \n            let icon = '';\n            let colorClass = 'text-gray-300';\n            \n            if (type === 'success') {\n                icon = '<svg class=\"w-3 h-3 container.removeChild(container.lastChild);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Add opportunity\n        function addOpportunity(opp) {\n            const container = See result in Activity Log\n\n### Adjusting Settings\n\nClick **Settings** to modify:\n\n**Min Profit Threshold:**\n- Lower (0.5%) = More opportunities, smaller profits\n- Higher (2%) = Fewer opportunities, bigger profits\n\n**Trade Amount:**\n- Start small ($10-25)\n- Scale up as you gain confidence\n- Never exceed your wallet balance!\n\n**Poll Interval:**\n- Faster (10s) = More API calls, catch opportunities quicker\n- Slower (60s) = Less load, might miss fast opportunities\n- Default (30s) = Good balance\n\n---\n\n## \ud83d\udd27 Troubleshooting\n\n### Dashboard shows \"Disconnected\"\n\n**Problem:** Can't connect to API server\n\n**Solutions:**\n```bash\n# 1. Check if API server is running\n# You should see it running in a terminal\n\n# 2. Restart the API server\npython api_server.py\n\n# 3. Check firewall/antivirus\n# Make sure localhost:5000 is allowed\n```\n\n### Dashboard loads but bot won't start\n\n**Check the Activity Log for errors:**\n\n**\"Bot not initialized\"**\n```bash\n# Make sure .env file is configured\ncat .env  # Check your private key is there\n```\n\n**\"No markets loaded\"**\n```bash\n# Run market discovery first\npython discover_markets.py\n```\n\n**\"Not enough balance/allowance\"**\n```bash\n# Set token allowances\npython setup_allowances.py\n```\n\n### Opportunities found but no trades executing\n\n**Check your settings:**\n1. Is `AUTO_EXECUTE=true` in your .env?\n2. Is your wallet funded with USDC?\n3. Is Trade Amount set appropriately?\n\n**Check the logs:**\n```bash\n# Look at the API server terminal\n# It will show detailed error messages\n```\n\n### Stats not updating\n\n**Refresh your browser:**\n- Press F5 or Cmd+R\n- Clear cache: Ctrl+Shift+R (Windows) or Cmd+Shift+R (Mac)\n\n**Check WebSocket connection:**\n- Look for \"Connected to server\" in Activity Log\n- Green dot next to \"API: Connected\"\n\n---\n\n## \ud83d\udca1 Pro Tips\n\n### 1. Run on Multiple Monitors\n- Put dashboard on one screen\n- Terminal logs on another\n- Watch opportunities in real-time!\n\n### 2. Mobile Monitoring\nIf you set up a proper HTTP server, you can access from your phone:\n```bash\n# Find your local IP\n# Mac/Linux: ifconfig | grep inet\n# Windows: ipconfig\n\n# Access from phone on same WiFi:\n# http://YOUR_LOCAL_IP:8080/dashboard.html\n```\n\n### 3. Keep it Running 24/7\n```bash\n# Use screen or tmux\nscreen -S polymarket\npython api_server.py\n# Press Ctrl+A, then D to detach\n\n# Reattach later\nscreen -r polymarket\n```\n\n### 4. Set Up Notifications\nAdd this to your .env:\n```bash\n# Get Slack webhook from slack.com/apps\nSLACK_WEBHOOK_URL=your_webhook_url_here\n```\n\nThe bot will send you notifications when trades execute!\n\n### 5. Track Performance\nAll trades are logged to `trades.jsonl`:\n```bash\n# View your trade history\ncat trades.jsonl | python -m json.tool\n\n# Calculate total profit\ncat trades.jsonl | grep profit | awk '{sum+=$2} END {print sum}'\n```\n\n---\n\n## \ud83c\udfa8 Customization\n\n### Change Colors\nEdit `dashboard.html`, find the color classes:\n- `from-indigo-500` = Primary color\n- `from-green-500` = Success/profit color\n- `from-red-500` = Error/stop color\n\nReplace with any Tailwind color!\n\n### Add More Stats\nIn `api_server.py`, add to `bot_state['stats']`:\n```python\nbot_state['stats']['your_new_stat'] = 0\n```\n\nThen in `dashboard.html`, add a new stat card.\n\n### Dark/Light Mode\nThe dashboard is dark mode by default.
